< review>
Terrible experience renting here. When I rented I was never informed that rent increases would happen. I had two rent increases happen in less then a year. The property is run down with building staircases missing steps and has many safety hazards. Units have no light inside of them and are pitch dark. The exit gate has also broken down multiple times and seems to keep breaking down repeatedly. I contacted the upper management, but nothing seems to have been done about fixing the property the whole time I rented. I mentioned my rent increases to upper management and they did not give me a rent decrease. This is despite me paying a higher price than the price of a bigger storage unit than mine after rent increases went through.

They told me my only option was I would have to transfer all my items into another unit to get a unit of a cheaper price. Horrible business practice. The office staff is good, but the property itself and the company is abysmal. They do not seem to care about their properties or customers. Typical company that cares only about money and puts customers second. This company would rather get a new customer than maintain good loyal customers who follow the rules and pay on time. Absolutely backwards way to run a business.</review>

< Text>
This property has a lot of great outdoor spaces. My stepson rented here a few weeks back and I am helping him move some items as he's in the middle of a move. The staff manager who works here Michael I always see cleaning around the buildings. He also helped me out when I got stuck outside the gate and didn't know how to put the code into the keypad properly. I had forgotten to press the star before I typed the numbers in for the code. If Michael hadn't helped me I would have been stuck for a long time trying to figure out the gate system. Thank you to Michael for helping me out you are a life saver.</Text>

< Review>
Office staff (Kit) was very friendly and professional. Kit answered all our questions and showed us two units so we could choose.  We rented a unit the same day.  Location is very clean albeit older than the location we were used to on Miramar Road.  The Solana Beach location does not have climate control and the doors to the (interior) unit are not metal and do not roll up.  It is more like a home closet (swing) door.  Nevertheless, we are happy with the location and recommend it.</Review>

<Review>I have rented five or six times over the last seven years at Stevens Ave. Public Storage.  I have found this facility to be excellent.  The facility is clean, well maintained, secure, and easy to navigate with no surprises.

The staff has always been, professional, helpful, and friendly.  Juana the manager has been there for several years and has always been very enjoyable to work with.

Based on my consistently good experiences at the Stevens Avenue location, I would not hesitate to check with Public Storage first if I would ever need to rent at another location.

Customers should know that Public Storage does require renters insurance with the storage facility address listed as an insured location.  You can either buy insurance there, or arrange for it with your homeowners insurance.

Last time I priced rental coverage with my homeowners insurance, it saved me $5.00 dollars over the insurance sold at Public Storage for a short-term rental.   I just bought the public storage insurance, because I did not want to spend a 1/2 hour more on the phone with my insurance agency answering policy questions.   For longer term rentals, you may be able to save more money by adding the rental location to your home owners policy.

You will also need a Public Storage approved lock.   One of their approved locks is a round shielded shackle padlock.   They sell them for $15 on Amazon.  I bought mine at Public Storage years ago, and don't remember what I paid for it.   I think it was within a couple dollars of the Amazon price though.  [Update] Actually, I just look on the PS website and saw that their locks are a couple bucks cheaper than Amazon!

It is also very easy to reserve units online.  I have done this almost every time I have rented with them.  They have a variety of incentives on various sizes of storage lockers.  Do the math and you can find which incentive works best for your anticipated rental term.

While I have not rented with any other company, over the years I have occasionally shopped the competition, and also have gone with friends to their storage rental facilities.   I have never come across another company that offers more value than Public Storage.

I do not hesitate to recommend Public Storage.   For my needs their combination of location, facilities, and price is unbeatable.<//Review>< Rate>
5</Rate>

<Text>Restaurant week in Newport Beach is a special event  we have enjoyed for many years and we had been looking forward to having some great dinners and supporting our local restaurants after the long Pandemic.  We had confirmed reservations for 7:30pm for a table of 4 persons and arrived precisely on schedule for our reservation and were seated immediately without delay.  Within a few minutes our waitress arrived.  We explained that we have a wine cellar and brought a special bottle from our cellar to enjoy &  offered to pay the corkage fee.  I asked if they had a decanter.  She told us they had decanters and a few minutes later she returned to announce they were all being cleaned and none were available  for us so they would "waive" the corkage fee.  She said she was going to attend to one other table and be back to answer any quiestions we had about the special selections for the evening.  She did not return.  After 45 minutes we flagged her down and she came over and asked abruptly, "So what do you want to order?."  We quickly made our selections.  30 minutes later 2 salads and one bowl of luke-warm soup arrived.  A cold breeze kept blowing out the outside propane heaters and it was uncomfortably cold. At 9:15 we had been seated for one hour and forty-five minutes and our food had not arrived, and more importantly, we had not received a visit to our table by the waitress or the restaurant owners to address the issue of no food in almost two hours.  We had to wave down our waitress to find out what was the problem.  During this time, it was obvious that other guests at adjacent tables had completely eaten their meals and left.   We did notice however that several other people who had waited for more than an hour simply left before receiving any food.  At 9:30, after having spent 2 hours and still getting nothing more than the initial salad an hour earlier, we confronted our waitress who said, "The kitchen is just really busy."  We had not ordered anything unusual, merely the items off the Restaurant Week fixed menu.  In disgust, we departed at 9:30 having never received our food.  We are all well-behaved, appropriately attired, retired local people in our mid-60's and we are not accustomed to such service.  We have enjoyed dining in Newport Beach at the wonderful water-front restaurants for more than 30 years. We have enjoyed visiting several local Newport Beach restaurants for this year's Restaurant Week promotion.   In that entire time we have never experienced the disappointment and poor service we had at the Bayside Restaurant. You would be well advised to find alternative dinner accommodations so you too are not disappointed.   Life is simply too short to tolerate such conduct with so many wonderful and delightful restaurants in the immediate area.< /Text>< pics>

< text>
My overall experience was disappointing. It's pretty embarrassing really for how expensive the meals are and given the nice location in Newport.
I ordered the rib-eye medium rare. It was more like medium/med well and my jaw was tired chewing the tough meat... I also could've done without the reduction sauce which tasted like sour cream mostly. Mashed potatoes were okay I guess.
My girlfriend ordered shrimp risotto. The rice was sort of dry for risotto as it didn't have a sufficient amount of the creaminess to flavor the rice. To top it all off, the shrimp were overcooked....
I had high expectations paying $50 for a steak dinner. I was so disappointed.
Lastly, the service was average at best. I sort of expected more from the upscale environment the restaurant gave off.
This meal almost ruined my night.<//text>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
I've been here a couple times and can say that many aspects of this restaurant are awesome. For starters, their service is very good and as long as a reservation is made it's a pretty quick sit-down upon arrival. On weekends they play live music on one side of the restaurant which makes it kind of nice; great date spot. The average age of the people dining here is definitely 45+ but still quite fun. Decent wine selection. Their food is very good. Their oysters are fresh. They have a beet salad which is mixed with some cream cheese and walnuts and is very tasty. Their fish is obviously very good but their filet mignon was also very well done. The filet migon come with a side of 3 different types of potato which is unique, mashed, a fried big potato chip and some roasted potatoes. All in all great experience and highly recommend going here with family or a special date night.<//Review>

<user>113897371292918169007< /user><username>Ian - Fr0wnZ<//username><time>1406775311758</time>< rating>

< review>
I came here to end my Orange County Restaurant Week experience and it was a fine choice! The restaurant is secluded adjacent from some beautiful housing and apartment complexes. There is a waterfront view if you're seated outside or by the window. I made reservations for two because this is quite a popular restaurant and it had to be as perfect evening out. That night the restaurant also provided complimentary valet. What an added bonus!

The ambiance was excellent, however; the seating arrangement we had was little odd. I prefer to sit across from someone rather seating side by side, but whatever. We started off with a little wine -- Pinot & Chardonnay, then it was off to ordering off the selected pre-fixed menu.

Food --
1st Course:
- Soup of the Day: Chicken Barley, which was a bit on the salty side but it was alright. I added some water to dilute the saltiness.
- Anjou Pear Salad: Beautifully presented. Love the display on the plate and very colorful. I made the wrong choice, but luckily we shared.

2nd Course:
- Tiger Prawns: This was supposed to my dish since I love seafood but this had the attention of my date, so why not. The prawns were served with a delicious risotto! Wow loved that dish.
- Prime Culotte Steak: If you're a meat lover, this dish is for you. It was served with blue cheese potato fondue and asparagus. Although this dish was excellent, the prawns was much better in my opinion.

3rd Course:
Selection of any dessert on the list
- Panna Cotta w/ Raspberries: Delicious! Creamy, sweet texture and the portion was very generous.
- NO Bread Pudding: Date loved this. The restaurant was also nice enough to add candles and decoration to make it extra special. It's very rich, so watch out.

Overall, this has become one of my favorite restaurants in Newport Beach. Location, atmosphere, price, food, and service deserve high remarks. Come hungry because portions are a nice size. Definitely recommend this spot to anyone!</review>

< text>
The crew is VERY polite, and they do their best.

I've been asked to pull over in drive thru once, and I had to go inside to ask about my order. Turns out they forgot about it, so I just asked for a refund.

Today I ordered the popcorn chicken with curly fries. It wasn't bad, but KFC does it better. I'd only order it again for the spicy chicken.

I didn't eat the curly fries because they were stale. Which was a bummer, the curly fries are usually always good, but these had the taste and texture of fries that were left out and then reheated ðŸ¤¢ I even separated them from the chicken they were so gross

I still like Jack in the Box, but I definitely have to think about coming back to this one.<//text>

When I go up to pay my bill (I am in the drive thru) my bill is $7.96! A difference of $2.10 (not including tax). I get to my office and realize I did not get the bacon and the home fries which they charged me 70 cents for is only a large tablespoon full in a side container. I called and asked to speak to a Manager. There isn't one. I'm told to come back "whenever" and they will give me my food. How did we go from $5.29 to $7.96?
